Introduction

This is a report for the insert benchmark with 800M docs and 4 client(s). It is generated by scripts (bash, awk, sed) and Tufte might not be impressed. An overview of the insert benchmark is here and a short update is here. Below, by DBMS, I mean DBMS+version.config. An example is my8020.c10b40 where my means MySQL, 8020 is version 8.0.20 and c10b40 is the name for the configuration file.

The test server has 8 AMD cores, 16G RAM and an NVMe SSD. It is described here as the Beelink. The benchmark was run with 4 clients and there were 1 or 3 connections per client (1 for queries or inserts without rate limits, 1+1 for rate limited inserts+deletes). It uses 4 tables with a table per client. It loads 800M rows per table without secondary indexes, creates 3 secondary indexes per table, then inserts 2m rows per table with a delete per insert to avoid growing the table. It then does 6 read+write tests for 1800s each that do queries as fast as possible with 100,100,500,500,1000,1000 inserts/s and the same for deletes/s per client concurrent with the queries. The database is larger than memory. Clients and the DBMS share one server. The per-database configs are in the per-database subdirectories here.

The tested DBMS are:

  • ma100244_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.2.44 with the cz11a_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT_NO_FSYNC
  • ma100244_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.2.44 with the cz11apur1_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT_NO_FSYNC, innodb_purge_threads=1
  • ma100339_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.3.39 with the cz11a_bee config
  • ma100339_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.3.39 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • ma100433_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.4.33 with the cz11a_bee config
  • ma100433_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.4.33 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • ma100524_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.5.24 with the cz11a_bee config
  • ma100524_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.5.24 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • ma100617_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.6.17 with the cz11a_bee config
  • ma100617_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.6.17 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • ma101107_rel.cz11a_bee - MariaDB 10.11.7 with the cz11a_bee config
  • ma101107_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MariaDB 10.11.7 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • ma101107_rel.cz11b_bee - MariaDB 10.11.7 with the cz11b_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT
  • ma101107_rel.cz11c_bee - MariaDB 10.11.7 with the cz11c_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=fsync
  • ma110401_rel.cz11b_bee - MariaDB 11.4.1 with the cz11b_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT
  • ma110401_rel.cz11bpur1_bee - MariaDB 11.4.1 with the cz11bpur1_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT, innodb_purge_threads=1
  • ma110401_rel.cz11c_bee - MariaDB 11.4.1 with the cz11c_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=fsync
  • my5651_rel.cz11a_bee - MySQL 5.6.51 with the cz11a_bee config
  • my5744_rel.cz11a_bee - MySQL 5.7.44 with the cz11a_bee config
  • my5744_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MySQL 5.7.44 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • my8036_rel.cz11a_bee - MySQL 8.0.36 with the cz11a_bee config
  • my8036_rel.cz11apur1_bee - MySQL 8.0.36 with the cz11apur1_bee config
  • my8036_rel.cz11b_bee - MySQL 8.0.36 with the cz11b_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=O_DIRECT
  • my8036_rel.cz11c_bee - MySQL 8.0.36 with the cz11c_bee config that uses innodb_flush_method=fsync
  • my8036_rel.cz11d_bee - MySQL 8.0.36 with the cz11d_bee config that uses innodb_change_buffering=none
  • pg162_def.cx9a2_bee - Postgres 16.2 with the cx9a2_bee config

Summary

The numbers are inserts/s for l.i0, l.i1 and l.i2, indexed docs (or rows) /s for l.x and queries/s for qr100, qp100 thru qr1000, qp1000" The values are the average rate over the entire test for inserts (IPS) and queries (QPS). The range of values for IPS and QPS is split into 3 parts: bottom 25%, middle 50%, top 25%. Values in the bottom 25% have a red background, values in the top 25% have a green background and values in the middle have no color. A gray background is used for values that can be ignored because the DBMS did not sustain the target insert rate. Red backgrounds are not used when the minimum value is within 80% of the max value.
